get_lang(){global$ca;return$ca;}function
lang($u,$xf=null){if(is_string($u)){$yg=array_search($u,get_translations("en"));if($yg!==false)$u=$yg;}global$ca,$Ri;$Qi=($Ri[$u]?$Ri[$u]:$u);if(is_array($Qi)){$yg=($xf==1?0:($ca=='cs'||$ca=='sk'?($xf&&$xf<5?1:2):($ca=='fr'?(!$xf?0:1):($ca=='pl'?($xf%10>1&&$xf%10<5&&$xf/10%10!=1?1:2):($ca=='sl'?($xf%100==1?0:($xf%100==2?1:($xf%100==3||$xf%100==4?2:3))):($ca=='lt'?($xf%10==1&&$xf%100!=11?0:($xf%10>1&&$xf/10%10!=1?1:2)):($ca=='bs'||$ca=='ru'||$ca=='sr'||$ca=='uk'?($xf%10==1&&$xf%100!=11?0:($xf%10>1&&$xf%10<5&&$xf/10%10!=1?1:2)):1)))))));$Qi=$Qi[$yg];}$Fa=func_get_args();array_shift($Fa);$yd=str_replace("%d","%s",$Qi);if($yd!=$Qi)$Fa[0]=format_number($xf);return

switch_lang(){global$ca,$Ee;echo"<form action='' method='post'>\n<div id='lang'>",lang(19).": ".html_select("lang",$Ee,$ca,"this.form.submit();")," <input type='submit' value='".lang(20)."' class='hidden'>\n","<input type='hidden' name='token' value='".get_token()."'>\n";echo"</div>\n</form>\n";}if(isset($_POST["lang"])&&verify_token()){cookie("adminer_lang",$_POST["lang"]);$_SESSION["lang"]=$_POST["lang"];$_SESSION["translations"]=array();redirect(remove_from_uri());}$ca="en";if(isset($Ee[$_COOKIE["adminer_lang"]])){cookie("adminer_lang",$_COOKIE["adminer_lang"]);$ca=$_COOKIE["adminer_lang"];}elseif(isset($Ee[$_SESSION["lang"]]))$ca=$_SESSION["lang"];else{$xa=array();preg_match_all('~([-a-z]+)(;q=([0-9.]+))?~',str_replace("_","-",strtolower($_SERVER["HTTP_ACCEPT_LANGUAGE"])),$Ve,PREG_SET_ORDER);foreach($Ve
